-- DROP TABLE core."role";

CREATE TABLE core."role" (
	id uuid NOT NULL,
	create_date timestamp NOT NULL,
	update_date timestamp NOT NULL,
	last_modified_by varchar(100) NULL,
	created_by varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	record_status varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	role_scope varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	"name" varchar(256) NOT NULL,
	normalized_name varchar(256) NULL,
	concurrency_stamp varchar(450) NULL,
	can_see_sensitive_data bool DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT pk_role PRIMARY KEY (id)
);
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX "RoleNameIndex" ON core.role USING btree (normalized_name);
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX ix_role_name ON core.role USING btree (name);{

-- core.role_claim definition

-- Drop table

-- DROP TABLE core.role_claim;

CREATE TABLE core.role_claim (
	id int4 GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY( INCREMENT BY 1 MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 2147483647 START 1 CACHE 1 NO CYCLE) NOT NULL,
	create_date timestamp NOT NULL,
	update_date timestamp NOT NULL,
	last_modified_by varchar(100) NULL,
	created_by varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	record_status varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	role_id uuid NOT NULL,
	claim_type text NULL,
	claim_value text NULL,
	CONSTRAINT pk_role_claim PRIMARY KEY (id)
);
CREATE INDEX ix_role_claim_role_id ON core.role_claim USING btree (role_id);


-- core.role_claim foreign keys

ALTER TABLE core.role_claim ADD CONSTRAINT fk_role_claim_role_role_id FOREIGN KEY (role_id) REFERENCES core."role"(id) ON DELETE CASCADE;

-- core.role_screen definition

-- Drop table

-- DROP TABLE core.role_screen;

CREATE TABLE core.role_screen (
	id uuid NOT NULL,
	role_id uuid NOT NULL,
	screen_id uuid NOT NULL,
	create_date timestamp NOT NULL,
	update_date timestamp NULL,
	created_by varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	last_modified_by varchar(50) NULL,
	record_status varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT pk_role_screen PRIMARY KEY (id)
);
CREATE INDEX ix_role_screen_role_id ON core.role_screen USING btree (role_id);
CREATE INDEX ix_role_screen_screen_id ON core.role_screen USING btree (screen_id);


-- core.role_screen foreign keys

ALTER TABLE core.role_screen ADD CONSTRAINT fk_role_screen_roles_role_id FOREIGN KEY (role_id) REFERENCES core."role"(id) ON DELETE CASCADE;
ALTER TABLE core.role_screen ADD CONSTRAINT fk_role_screen_screen_screen_id FOREIGN KEY (screen_id) REFERENCES core.screen(id) ON DELETE CASCADE;

-- core.screen definition

-- Drop table

-- DROP TABLE core.screen;

CREATE TABLE core.screen (
	id uuid NOT NULL,
	"name" varchar(100) NOT NULL,
	"module" varchar(100) NOT NULL,
	operation_type varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	create_date timestamp NOT NULL,
	update_date timestamp NULL,
	created_by varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	last_modified_by varchar(50) NULL,
	record_status varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	icon text NULL,
	link text NULL,
	module_icon text NULL,
	module_link text NULL,
	module_priority int4 DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
	priority int4 DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT pk_screen PRIMARY KEY (id)
);

-- core.screen_claim definition

-- Drop table

-- DROP TABLE core.screen_claim;

CREATE TABLE core.screen_claim (
	id uuid NOT NULL,
	screen_id uuid NOT NULL,
	claim_value text NULL,
	create_date timestamp NOT NULL,
	update_date timestamp NULL,
	created_by varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	last_modified_by varchar(50) NULL,
	record_status varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT pk_screen_claim PRIMARY KEY (id)
);
CREATE INDEX ix_screen_claim_screen_id ON core.screen_claim USING btree (screen_id);


-- core.screen_claim foreign keys

ALTER TABLE core.screen_claim ADD CONSTRAINT fk_screen_claim_screen_screen_id FOREIGN KEY (screen_id) REFERENCES core.screen(id) ON DELETE CASCADE;

-- core."user" definition

-- Drop table

-- DROP TABLE core."user";

CREATE TABLE core."user" (
	id uuid NOT NULL,
	first_name varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	last_name varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	identity_number varchar(50) NULL,
	birth_date timestamp NOT NULL,
	user_type varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	user_status varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	phone_code varchar(10) NOT NULL,
	create_date timestamp NOT NULL,
	update_date timestamp NOT NULL,
	last_modified_by varchar(100) NULL,
	created_by varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	password_modified_date timestamp NOT NULL,
	record_status varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	login_last_activity_id uuid NULL,
	user_name varchar(256) NULL,
	normalized_user_name varchar(256) NULL,
	email varchar(256) NULL,
	normalized_email varchar(256) NULL,
	email_confirmed bool NOT NULL,
	password_hash text NULL,
	security_stamp text NULL,
	concurrency_stamp text NULL,
	phone_number varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	phone_number_confirmed bool NOT NULL,
	two_factor_enabled bool NOT NULL,
	lockout_end timestamptz NULL,
	lockout_enabled bool NOT NULL,
	access_failed_count int4 NOT NULL,
	external_customer_id varchar(400) NULL,
	external_person_id varchar(400) NULL,
	aml_reference_number varchar(150) NULL,
	CONSTRAINT pk_user PRIMARY KEY (id)
);
CREATE INDEX "EmailIndex" ON core."user" USING btree (normalized_email);
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX "UserNameIndex" ON core."user" USING btree (normalized_user_name);
CREATE INDEX ix_user_email ON core."user" USING btree (email);
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX ix_user_identity_number ON core."user" USING btree (identity_number);
CREATE INDEX ix_user_phone_number ON core."user" USING btree (phone_number);
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX ix_user_user_name ON core."user" USING btree (user_name);
CREATE INDEX ix_user_user_status ON core."user" USING btree (user_status);
CREATE INDEX ix_user_user_type ON core."user" USING btree (user_type);

-- core.user_claim definition

-- Drop table

-- DROP TABLE core.user_claim;

CREATE TABLE core.user_claim (
	id int4 GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY( INCREMENT BY 1 MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 2147483647 START 1 CACHE 1 NO CYCLE) NOT NULL,
	description varchar(450) NULL,
	display_name varchar(450) NULL,
	create_date timestamp NOT NULL,
	update_date timestamp NOT NULL,
	last_modified_by varchar(100) NULL,
	created_by varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	record_status varchar(50) NOT NULL,
	user_id uuid NOT NULL,
	claim_type text NULL,
	claim_value text NULL,
	CONSTRAINT pk_user_claim PRIMARY KEY (id)
);
CREATE INDEX ix_user_claim_user_id ON core.user_claim USING btree (user_id);


-- core.user_claim foreign keys

ALTER TABLE core.user_claim ADD CONSTRAINT fk_user_claim_user_user_id FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES core."user"(id) ON DELETE CASCADE;

-- core.user_role definition

-- Drop table

-- DROP TABLE core.user_role;

CREATE TABLE core.user_role (
	user_id uuid NOT NULL,
	role_id uuid NOT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT pk_user_role PRIMARY KEY (user_id, role_id)
);
CREATE INDEX ix_user_role_role_id ON core.user_role USING btree (role_id);


-- core.user_role foreign keys

ALTER TABLE core.user_role ADD CONSTRAINT fk_user_role_role_role_id FOREIGN KEY (role_id) REFERENCES core."role"(id) ON DELETE CASCADE;
ALTER TABLE core.user_role ADD CONSTRAINT fk_user_role_user_user_id FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES core."user"(id) ON DELETE CASCADE;
